LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [i0].[Id], [i0].[TransactionId], [i0].[ProductId], [i0].[Quantity], [i0].[UnitPrice], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[CategoryId], [t0].[Name], [t0].[ProductCode], [t0].[PurchasePrice], [t0].[SellingPrice], [t0].[Status], [t0].[StockQuantity], [t0].[Unit]
    FROM [InventoryTransactionDetails] AS [i0]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CategoryId], [t].[Name], [t].[ProductCode], [t].[PurchasePrice], [t].[SellingPrice], [t].[Status], [t].[StockQuantity], [t].[Unit]
        FROM (
            SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductCode], [p].[PurchasePrice], [p].[SellingPrice], [p].[Status], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[Unit], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [p].[Id] ORDER BY [p].[Id]) AS [row]
            FROM [Products] AS [p]
        ) AS [t]
        WHERE [t].[row] <= 1
    ) AS [t0] ON [i0].[ProductId] = [t0].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [i].[Id] = [t1].[TransactionId]
